document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    const stickyElement = document.querySelector('[data-sticky]');
    const headerContentBlock = document.querySelector('.ct-header-content-block');

    if (stickyElement && headerContentBlock) {
        window.addEventListener("scroll", function () {

                headerContentBlock.style.display = "block";

                headerContentBlock.style.display = "none";

});

  opacity: 0; cursor: pointer; z-index: 999;
}

  background: #470c62; color: #fff;
  padding: 12px 14px 12px 46px; /* space for chevron */

  border-bottom: 1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.18);
}

  content: "";
  position: absolute; left: 16px; top: 50%;
  width: 10px; height: 10px;
  border-right: 2px solid #fff;
  border-top:   2px solid #fff;
  transform: translateY(-50%) rotate(45deg); /* ▶ */
  transition: transform .25s ease;
}

  transform: translateY(-50%) rotate(135deg); /* ▼ */

<script>
(function () {
  if (typeof window.gtag !== 'function') return;

  const els = document.querySelectorAll('a[data-banner-id="indian-film-festival"]');
  if (!els.length) return;

  els.forEach((el) => {
    let fired = false;
    let visibleTimer = null;

    const sendImpression = () => {
      if (fired) return;
      fired = true;
      window.gtag('event', 'banner_impression', {
        banner_id: el.dataset.bannerId,
        banner_position: el.dataset.bannerPosition,
        campaign_name: el.dataset.campaignName
      });
    };

    const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
      const entry = entries[0];
      const ok = entry.isIntersecting && entry.intersectionRatio >= 0.5;

      if (ok) {
        if (!visibleTimer) {
          visibleTimer = setTimeout(() => {
            sendImpression();
            observer.disconnect();
          }, 1000);
        }
      } else {
        if (visibleTimer) {
          clearTimeout(visibleTimer);
          visibleTimer = null;
        }
      }
    }, { threshold: [0.5] });

    observer.observe(el);

    el.addEventListener('click', () => {
      window.gtag('event', 'banner_click', {
        banner_id: el.dataset.bannerId,
        banner_position: el.dataset.bannerPosition,
        campaign_name: el.dataset.campaignName
      });
    }, { passive: true });
  });
})();
</script></div>
